# Unified Gameplay Transcript

Loops are split by the in-game bells. Within each loop, the timestamp shown is **real recording time elapsed since the bells of the previous loop** (MM:SS, or H:MM:SS once an hour has passed).  When a loop spans a session break and the GM restarts the loop at the top of the next recording, the clock resets to 0:00 (matching the GM's in-game minute counter) and a divider notes the restart.
